If there is $100 million of debt and $200 million of CDS, and if the expected recovery on the debt is 25 cents on the dollar, then the CDS ‚Äúshould‚Äù pay out 75 cents on the dollar (for a total of $150 million). But if one seller sold all of that CDS, then it would prefer to pay $100 million for all of the debt (and zero on the CDS).
